[endif] Kumar Vishwas spoke to the media at his residence in Ghaziabad after the meeting on cmwas
 unka kahana tha ki bhrashtachar virdohi andolan ke liye mishra ke aarope behaddukhad hai
 According to Kumar, he has known Arvind Kejriwal for the last 12 years and he can never be corrupt
 kumaar vishwaas kaa maananaa he ki kejariwal ke dushman bhiunpar aisa aarope nahin laga sakate
 He also sought evidence on these allegations
 vishwaas kaa kahana tha ki agar kapil mishra ke paas vaaki aisi jaankaree thi to unhen yebaat party ke manch par saamne rakhni chahie thi
 Retweeting the tweet of Ekla Chalo re'kumar Vishwas, Kapil Mishra wrote, 'on the day Satyendra Jain goes to jail, you too will accept my brother
 tab tak "ekala chalo re
 "the day Satyendra Jain will go to jail, on that day you will also accept my brother
 tab tak "ekala chalo re"https: / / t
 co / uszcmk4fpc — Kapil Mishra (@kapilmishraaap) May 7, 2017 Yogendra Yadav also defends Aam Aadmi Party's former leader Yogendra Yadav has questioned Kapil Mishra
 yogendra yadavane saaf taur par kaha ki kejariwal kabhi ghoose nahin le sakate
 He said that such serious allegations should not be made in such light manner
 saath hi unhone ye bhi kaha ki kapil mishra ab tak kyon shant baithe the
 On the other hand, senior leader of the Aam Aadmi Party, Sanjay Singh also appeared in support of Kejriwal
 sanjay ne apane twit main likhaa, 'arvind kejariwal kii eemaandaaree par unka dushman bhi shaq nahin karata, mantri pad jane kii baukhalaahat main diya gaya kapil mishra kaa bayaan ghatiya or ochhaa he
 'let us tell you that on Sunday morning, former Minister Kapil Mishra accused Kejriwal of taking two crore rupees from Delhi Minister Satyendar Jain
 kapil ne kaha tha ki unhone shuukravaar ko apni ankhon ke saamne kejariwal ko paisa lete hue dekha tha
 Before the general election season arrives in the country, the central and state governments have once again started taking care of the farmers
 pehle centre ne ganna kisaanon ke liye badi raahat dete hue unka bakaayaa kaa bhugtan karne kaa elaan kiya, vahiin ab bihar ne mausam kii maar se pareshaan kisaanon ke hit ke liye rajya 'fasal sahaayta yojana' kii shuruyaat kar di he
 Chief Minister Nitish Kumar's ambitious state 'crop assistance scheme' will benefit lakhs of farmers in Bihar who are facing crop loss due to the weather
 isse pehle rajya main pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana chal rahi thi, lekin usamenkisanonko zyada muaavja nahin miltaa tha
 The state government has also launched a special crop insurance scheme for farmers in the name of 'inclusive Crop Assistance Scheme'
 is yojana ke lagu hone ke baad pradesh main pehle se jo bhi fasal beemaa yojanaayen chal rahi thim, uski jagah is nai yojana kii shuruyaat kii gai he
 After the defeat in the recent by-election, it is being considered as a big bet by the Nitish government in efforts to save its base
 vahiin centre ne bhi ganna kisaanon ke liye 8,500 karod rupee ke belout package dene kii yojana par apni manjuuri de di he
 How much benefit will be received Under the 'crop assistance scheme', the farmers of Bihar will be compensated by the state government for their crop failure
 yojana kaa laabh lene ke liye kisaanon ko prayek kharif or rabi kii fasal ke mausam main online portal par nibandhan karana hoga
 Under the scheme, if the actual yield rate of the crop is reduced by 20%, a maximum of 15 thousand rupees will be given at the rate of Rs 7,500 per hectare and maximum rupees 20 thousand rupees will be given at the rate of Rs 10 thousand per hectare for more than 20% damage
 is yojana kaa laabh raiyat yaa gaiyr raiyat donon tarah ke kisaan uthaa sakate hai
 To avail the benefit, the Ryot farmers will have to submit their land paper, while the non-ryat farmers will have to give a self-declaration, which will be approved by the farmer advisor or ward member
 bihar PM fasal beemaa yojana se baharmukhyamantri nitish kumaar kii adhyakshata main unke sarkari awaas par hui cabinet kii baithak ke dauraan is yojana par muhar lagi
 With this, Bihar has become the first state in the country to come out of the ambit of Pradhan Mantri Crop Insurance Scheme
 isse pehle pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana ke tahat centre ko 49 pratishat, rajya ko 49 pratishat or kisaan ko 2 pratishat premium raashi ke rup main hissaa bhugtan karnaa padataa tha, lekin iskaa phayda keval kuch rini kisaanon ko mil paata tha
 Principal Secretary of the State Cooperative Department, Atul Prasad said that according to the data of 2016, the premium amount of the state government under the Prime Minister's Crop Insurance Scheme was 495 crores while the relief amount given to the farmers was only 221 crores
 isi vajah se rajya ke sabhi varg ke kisaanon ko raahat pahunchane ke liye is nai samaveshi 'bihar rajya fasal sahaayta yojana' kii shuruyaat kii gai he
 With the introduction of this scheme, Bihar has become the first state where such a scheme has been introduced to provide relief to farmers on crop loss
 rajya sarkaar kii is nai yojana ke lagu ho jane ke baad pradesh main kisaanon ko phayda pahunchane ke liye pehle se chal rahe pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana or anya kisi prakaar kii beemaa yojana ab band ho jaaegi
 Writing the history of the twenty-first century, it must be recorded that China may not have changed as fast as the world changed about it
 baat isi sitambar kii he jab america main bhartiya pradhanmantri sahit lagbhag sabhi global rashtradhyaksh maujuud the lekin ahmiyat rakhane vaali nigahen keval china ke raashtrapati shi jinping kii america kii yatra par thim, jo yah sunishchit karne ke liye beijing pahunche the ki china kii mudra yuan (jise renminbi bhi kehete hai) ko karency ke us abhijatya club main shaamil kiya jayega jisamen ab tak keval america dollar, japani yen, british pound or euro ko jagah mili he
 The campaign, which floated in Washington's diplomatic corridors in September, became big news last fortnight when the IMF announced that its experts agreed on Yuan's entry into the SDR
 iske saath hi tay ho gaya ki aktubar 2016 main yuan ko duniya kii paanchavin sabase taqatvar karency banane kii aupchaarikta puri ho jaaegi
 The entry of the yuan into the SDR has given credibility to the world's second largest economy, which is unmatched
 videshi mudra sankat main fanse deshon ke liye iemef kii madad antim sahaara hoti he jo ki haal main greece yaa europe ke anya sankatagrast deshon ko or 1991 main bharat ko mili thi
 SDR i
e
 Special Drawing Rights is a crisis system under IMF
 esadiar ek tarah kii karency he jo iemef ke sadsy deshon ke videshi mudra bhandar ke hisse ke taur par gini jaati he
 In times of crisis, IMF gets resources instead
 esadiar ek takneekee intjaam he jisaki jarurat durbhaagya se hi padati he lekin paroksh rup se yah club darasal duniya ke videshi mudra bhandaron ke gathan kaa aadhaar he
 Forex reserves of almost all the countries of the world are based on dollar, yen, pound and euro, yuan will now be the fifth currency among them
 esadiar ne 46 saal ke itihaas main bahut kam surkhiyaan batori hai
 To get this status, the conditions of IMF are so difficult that no country looks at it
 2001 main kai europea mudraon ke vilay se bana euro iskaa hissaa bana tha
 There are two conditions for evaluating IMF for a currency
 pehali shart he ki is mudra ko jari karne vaala desh bada niryaatak hona chahie
 China is a major force on this scale with 11 per cent share in world exports
 niryaat ke paimaane par yuan dollar va euro ke baad tisare number par he, yen or pound kaaphi peeche hai
 The second condition of membership in the SDR club is that the currency can be used freely
 is paimaane par china shaayad khara nahin utarataa, kyonki yuan par paabandiyaan aayad hai or isaki keemat bhi bazaar nahin balki sarkaar tay karti he, lekin yah china kaa rasookh hi he ki iemef ne mukt karency ke paimaane par yuan ke liye paribhaasha badali he
 The IMF argues that the yuan's share in the international exchange is quite large
 2014 main yah vibhinn deshon ke mudra bhandaron main saatvin sabase badi karency thi
 The yuan is the 11th currency in global currency spot trading and the seventh largest in bond markets
 yahi vajah thi ki aparivartaneey hote hue bhi yuan ko vah darja mil gaya jo lagbhag asambhav he
 This height of the yuan will bring major changes
 esadiar main paanchavin karency aane ke saath agle kuch maheenon main duniya ke desh apane videshi mudra bhandaron kaa punargathan karenge or yuan kaa hissaa badhaaenge
 It is believed that about one trillion dollars of international foreign exchange reserves will be converted into yuan, that is, the demand for the yuan will also increase on the lines of the dollar
 valrd bank kaa maananaa he ki agle paanch saal main duniya kii companiyaan bade paimaane par yuan kendrit bond jari karengi, jinhen vittiya bazaar 'pandas bond' kahata he
 Their size can go up to $ 50 billion, which will increase its value manifold in financial markets
 yuan ne khud ko global rigerv karency banane kii taraf kadam badha diya he
 The impact of the British pound in global markets is limited, the Japanese yen is a collapsing currency and the future of the euro is volatile
 isliye america dollar or yuan shaayad duniya kii do sabase pramukh karency hongi
 Actually, this is what China wanted, so the coming of the yuan to the SDR is not just a financial event, but it will start the changes in the global economic-political balance that were being assessed for years
 darasal, yahaan se duniya main dollar ke ekadhikaar kii ulti ginati par bahes zyada tathy or thasak ke saath shuru ho rahi he, kyonki duniya ke kareeb 45 fisadi antaradeshy vinimay america dollar main hote hai jiske liye america banking system kii jarurat hoti he, jald hi iskaa ek bada hissaa yuan ko milegaa
 The status of the yuan is the most important step in the global economic power that China is on its way to becoming, but more important is that China has not changed as much as the world has changed towards China
